**Overview**\n\nThis scope of work details the **primer coat application process**, ensuring the stairway is properly prepped, dust-free, and ready for final painting. The process includes **pre-cleaning, priming, caulking, and drying periods** to achieve a smooth and durable base for the final coat.\n\n## **1 Paint-Ready Preparation**\n\n*    Ensure **all &quot;Final Prep Steps&quot;** are complete.\n    \n*    Verify that the **stairway is fully prepared for painting**, with surfaces sanded, cleaned, and dried.\n    \n\n## **2 Dust-Free &amp; Paint Application**\n\n*    Use a **Swiffer Sweeper** to **remove all remaining dust** before applying primer.\n    \n*    **Start from the top tread** and work downward, making sure:\n    \n    *   Each tread is **dust-free** before painting.\n        \n    *   Primer is applied **one tread at a time** before moving to the next.\n        \n\n## **3 Drying Period**\n\n*    **Allow at least 24 hours** for the primer to dry before proceeding.\n    \n\n## **4 Caulking Application**\n\n*    **Inspect the stairway** for any gaps or imperfections revealed by the primer coat.\n    \n*    Apply **&quot;Big Stretch&quot; caulking** to all areas requiring sealing.\n    \n\n## **5 Caulking Drying Period**\n\n*    **Wait at least 4 hours** to ensure the caulking is fully dry before continuing.\n    \n\n## **6 Final Preparation Before Color Coat**\n\n*    **Repeat Steps 1-3**, ensuring:\n    \n    *   The stairway is **dust-free** once again.\n        \n    *   A smooth, even **primer base** is achieved.\n        \n*    **Apply the final coat** using the selected **color and sheen** for the desired finish.\n    \n\n## ** Final Notes**\n\nThis structured approach ensures the **stairway is properly primed and prepped**before applying the final coat. Following **drying periods, dust removal, and caulking procedures** will result in a **flawless, professional-quality finish**.","html":"<h1 id=\"-scope-of-work-primer-coat\" class=\"op-uc-h1\"> <strong>Scope of Work: Primer Coat</strong><a class=\"op-uc-link_permalink icon-link op-uc-link\" aria-hidden=\"true\" href=\"#-scope-of-work-primer-coat\"></a>\n</h1>\n<h2 id=\"-overview\" class=\"op-uc-h2\"> <strong>Overview</strong><a class=\"op-uc-link_permalink icon-link op-uc-link\" aria-hidden=\"true\" href=\"#-overview\"></a>\n</h2>\n<p class=\"op-uc-p\">This scope of work details the <strong>primer coat application process</strong>, ensuring the stairway is properly prepped, dust-free, and ready for final painting.
